<li id="cite_note-vanderW2-12"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-vanderW2_12-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Iamblichus" title="Iamblichus">Iamblichus</a>, <i>Life of Pythagoras</i>,(trans., for example, <a href="#CITEREFGuthrie1987">Guthrie 1987</a>) cited in <a href="#CITEREFvan_der_Waerden1961">van der Waerden 1961</a>, p. 108. See also <a href="/wiki/Porphyry_(philosopher)" title="Porphyry (philosopher)">Porphyry</a>, <i>Life of Pythagoras</i>, paragraph 6, in <a href="#CITEREFGuthrie1987">Guthrie 1987</a>
Van der Waerden (<a href="#CITEREFvan_der_Waerden1961">van der Waerden 1961</a>, pp. 87–90) sustains the view that Thales knew Babylonian mathematics.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-stanencyc-13"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-stanencyc_13-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Herodotus (II. 81) and Isocrates (<i>Busiris</i> 28), cited in: <a href="#CITEREFHuffman2011">Huffman 2011</a>. On Thales, see Eudemus ap. Proclus, 65.7, (for example, <a href="#CITEREFMorrow1992">Morrow 1992</a>, p. 52) cited in: <a href="#CITEREFO'Grady2004">O'Grady 2004</a>, p. 1. Proclus was using a work by <a href="/wiki/Eudemus_of_Rhodes" title="Eudemus of Rhodes">Eudemus of Rhodes</a> (now lost), the <i>Catalogue of Geometers</i>. See also introduction, <a href="#CITEREFMorrow1992">Morrow 1992</a>, p. xxx on Proclus's reliability.</span>
</li>

<li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation journal cs1" id="CITEREFVardi1998">Vardi, Ilan (April 1998). <a class="external text" href="https://www.cs.drexel.edu/~crorres/Archimedes/Cattle/cattle_vardi.pdf" rel="nofollow">"Archimedes' Cattle Problem"</a> <span class="cs1-format">(PDF)</span>. <i>American Mathematical Monthly</i>. <b>105</b> (4): 305–19. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CiteSeerX_(identifier)" title="CiteSeerX (identifier)">CiteSeerX</a> <span class="cs1-lock-free" title="Freely accessible"><a class="external text" href="//citeseerx.ist.psu.edu/viewdoc/summary?doi=10.1.1.383.545" rel="nofollow">10.1.1.383.545</a></span>. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Doi_(identifier)" title="Doi (identifier)">doi</a>:<a class="external text" href="https://doi.org/10.2307%2F2589706" rel="nofollow">10.2307/2589706</a>. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/JSTOR_(identifier)" title="JSTOR (identifier)">JSTOR</a> <a class="external text" href="//www.jstor.org/stable/2589706" rel="nofollow">2589706</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=American+Mathematical+Monthly&amp;rft.atitle=Archimedes%27+Cattle+Problem&amp;rft.volume=105&amp;rft.issue=4&amp;rft.pages=305-19&amp;rft.date=1998-04&amp;rft_id=%2F%2Fciteseerx.ist.psu.edu%2Fviewdoc%2Fsummary%3Fdoi%3D10.1.1.383.545%23id-name%3DCiteSeerX&amp;rft_id=%2F%2Fwww.jstor.org%2Fstable%2F2589706%23id-name%3DJSTOR&amp;rft_id=info%3Adoi%2F10.2307%2F2589706&amp;rft.aulast=Vardi&amp;rft.aufirst=Ilan&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.cs.drexel.edu%2F~crorres%2FArchimedes%2FCattle%2Fcattle_vardi.pdf&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ANumber+theory"></span></li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Further_reading">Further reading</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Number_theory&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Further reading">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Two of the most popular introductions to the subject are:
</p>
<ul><li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation book cs1" id="CITEREFG.H._HardyE.M._Wright2008"><a href="/wiki/G._H._Hardy" title="G. H. Hardy">G.H. Hardy</a>; E.M. Wright (2008) [1938]. <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=rey9wfSaJ9EC" rel="nofollow"><i>An introduction to the theory of numbers</i></a> (rev. by D.R. Heath-Brown and J.H. Silverman, 6th ed.). <a href="/wiki/Oxford_University_Press" title="Oxford University Press">Oxford University Press</a>. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISBN_(identifier)" title="ISBN (identifier)">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-19-921986-5" title="Special:BookSources/978-0-19-921986-5"><bdi>978-0-19-921986-5</bdi></a><span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">2016-03-02</span></span>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=An+introduction+to+the+theory+of+numbers&amp;rft.edition=rev.+by+D.R.+Heath-Brown+and+J.H.+Silverman%2C+6th&amp;rft.pub=Oxford+University+Press&amp;rft.date=2008&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-19-921986-5&amp;rft.au=G.H.+Hardy&amp;rft.au=E.M.+Wright&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3Drey9wfSaJ9EC&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ANumber+theory"></span></li>
<li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation book cs1" id="CITEREFVinogradov2003"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ivan_Matveyevich_Vinogradov" title="Ivan Matveyevich Vinogradov">Vinogradov, I.M.</a> (2003) [1954]. <i>Elements of Number Theory</i> (reprint of the 1954 ed.). Mineola, NY: Dover Publications.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Elements+of+Number+Theory&amp;rft.place=Mineola%2C+NY&amp;rft.edition=reprint+of+the+1954&amp;rft.pub=Dover+Publications&amp;rft.date=2003&amp;rft.aulast=Vinogradov&amp;rft.aufirst=I.M.&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ANumber+theory"></span></li></ul>
<p>Hardy and Wright's book is a comprehensive classic, though its clarity sometimes suffers due to the authors' insistence on elementary methods (<a href="#CITEREFApostoln.d.">Apostol n.d.</a>).
Vinogradov's main attraction consists in its set of problems, which quickly lead to Vinogradov's own research interests; the text itself is very basic and close to minimal. Other popular first introductions are:
</p>
<ul><li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation book cs1" id="CITEREFIvan_M._NivenHerbert_S._ZuckermanHugh_L._Montgomery2008"><a href="/wiki/Ivan_M._Niven" title="Ivan M. Niven">Ivan M. Niven</a>; Herbert S. Zuckerman; <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hugh_L._Montgomery" title="Hugh L. Montgomery">Hugh L. Montgomery</a> (2008) [1960]. <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=V52HIcKguJ4C" rel="nofollow"><i>An introduction to the theory of numbers</i></a> (reprint of the 5th edition 1991 ed.). <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/John_Wiley_%26_Sons" title="John Wiley &amp; Sons">John Wiley &amp; Sons</a>. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISBN_(identifier)" title="ISBN (identifier)">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-81-265-1811-1" title="Special:BookSources/978-81-265-1811-1"><bdi>978-81-265-1811-1</bdi></a><span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">2016-02-28</span></span>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=An+introduction+to+the+theory+of+numbers&amp;rft.edition=reprint+of+the+5th+edition+1991&amp;rft.pub=John+Wiley+%26+Sons&amp;rft.date=2008&amp;rft.isbn=978-81-265-1811-1&amp;rft.au=Ivan+M.+Niven&amp;rft.au=Herbert+S.+Zuckerman&amp;rft.au=Hugh+L.+Montgomery&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3DV52HIcKguJ4C&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ANumber+theory"></span></li>
<li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation book cs1" id="CITEREFKenneth_H._Rosen2010">Kenneth H. Rosen (2010). <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=JqycRAAACAAJ" rel="nofollow"><i>Elementary Number Theory</i></a> (6th ed.). <a href="/wiki/Pearson_Education" title="Pearson Education">Pearson Education</a>. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISBN_(identifier)" title="ISBN (identifier)">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-321-71775-7" title="Special:BookSources/978-0-321-71775-7"><bdi>978-0-321-71775-7</bdi></a><span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">2016-02-28</span></span>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Elementary+Number+Theory&amp;rft.edition=6th&amp;rft.pub=Pearson+Education&amp;rft.date=2010&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-321-71775-7&amp;rft.au=Kenneth+H.+Rosen&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3DJqycRAAACAAJ&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ANumber+theory"></span></li></ul>
<p>Popular choices for a second textbook include:
</p>
<ul><li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation book cs1" id="CITEREFBorevichShafarevich1966"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Borevich" title="Borevich">Borevich, A. I.</a>; <a href="/wiki/Igor_Shafarevich" title="Igor Shafarevich">Shafarevich, Igor R.</a> (1966). <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=njgVUjjO-EAC" rel="nofollow"><i>Number theory</i></a>. Pure and Applied Mathematics. Vol. 20. Boston, MA: <a href="/wiki/Academic_Press" title="Academic Press">Academic Press</a>. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISBN_(identifier)" title="ISBN (identifier)">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-12-117850-5" title="Special:BookSources/978-0-12-117850-5"><bdi>978-0-12-117850-5</bdi></a>. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MR_(identifier)" title="MR (identifier)">MR</a> <a class="external text" href="//www.ams.org/mathscinet-getitem?mr=0195803" rel="nofollow">0195803</a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Number+theory&amp;rft.place=Boston%2C+MA&amp;rft.series=Pure+and+Applied+Mathematics&amp;rft.pub=Academic+Press&amp;rft.date=1966&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-12-117850-5&amp;rft_id=%2F%2Fwww.ams.org%2Fmathscinet-getitem%3Fmr%3D0195803%23id-name%3DMR&amp;rft.aulast=Borevich&amp;rft.aufirst=A.+I.&amp;rft.au=Shafarevich%2C+Igor+R.&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3DnjgVUjjO-EAC&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ANumber+theory"></span></li>
<li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation book cs1" id="CITEREFSerre1996"><a href="/wiki/Jean-Pierre_Serre" title="Jean-Pierre Serre">Serre, Jean-Pierre</a> (1996) [1973]. <a class="external text" href="https://archive.org/details/courseinarithmet00serr" rel="nofollow"><i>A course in arithmetic</i></a>. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Graduate_texts_in_mathematics" title="Graduate texts in mathematics">Graduate texts in mathematics</a>. Vol. 7. Springer. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ISBN_(identifier)" title="ISBN (identifier)">ISBN</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-387-90040-7" title="Special:BookSources/978-0-387-90040-7"><bdi>978-0-387-90040-7</bdi></a>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=A+course+in+arithmetic&amp;rft.series=Graduate+texts+in+mathematics&amp;rft.pub=Springer&amp;rft.date=1996&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-387-90040-7&amp;rft.aulast=Serre&amp;rft.aufirst=Jean-Pierre&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Farchive.org%2Fdetails%2Fcourseinarithmet00serr&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ANumber+theory"></span></li></ul>
